targetTX {\n266\t\t\t\tm.txCount++\n267\t\t\t\tm.txNodes = append(m.txNodes, mac)\n268\t\t\t\treturn \"tx\"\n269\t\t\t}\n270\t\t\treturn \"rx\"\n271\t\t}\n272\t}\n273\t\n274\t// rebalanceRoles single-node mode)\n//   - 2 nodes: one TX, one RX (alternating by join order)\n//   - 3+ nodes: floor(N/2) nodes assigned TX, rest RX, staggered TX slots\nfunc (m *Manager) assignRole(mac string) string {\n\tm.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tn := len(m.online)\n\tswitch {\n\tcase n <= 1:\n\t\treturn \"tx_rx\"\n\tcase n == 2:\n\t\t// First to arrive is TX, second is RX.\n\t\tif m.txCount == 0 {\n\t\t\tm.txCount++\n\t\t\tm.txNodes = append(m.txNodes, mac)\n\t\t\treturn \"tx\"\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn \"rx\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\t// Keep TX count at floor(N/2), promote this node to TX if needed.\n\t\ttargetTX := n / 2\n\t\tif len(m.txNodes) < targetTX {\n\t\t\tm.txCount++\n\t\t\tm.txNodes = append(m.txNodes, mac)\n\t\t\treturn \"tx\"\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn \"rx\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// pairs\nfunc (cd *CollisionDetector) GetCollisionHistory(limit int) []CollisionEvent {\n\tcd.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer cd.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tvar allEvents []CollisionEvent\n\tfor _, events := range cd.collisionHistory {\n\t\tallEvents = append(allEvents, events...)\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort by timestamp descending\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(allEvents); i++ {\n\t\tfor j := i + 1; j < len(allEvents); j++ {\n\t\tallEvents = allEvents[:limit]\n\t}\n\n\treturn allEvents\n}\n\n// GenerateRestaggerOffset generates a new random stagger offset for a TX node\n// This shifts one node's slot by a fraction of the slot width to break up collisions\nfunc GenerateRestaggerOffset(txIndex, numTXNodes int, rateHz int) int {\n\t// Calculate slot width in microseconds\n\tslotWidthUS := 1_000_000 / (rateHz * numTXNodes)\n\n\t// Shift by a random fraction of the slot width (between 10% and 90%)\n\t// This ensures nodes don't all align at the same time\n\tfraction := 0.1 + rand.Float64()*0.8\n\tshiftUS := int(float64(slotWidthUS) * fraction)\n\n\t// Calculate the base offset for this TX node\n\tbaseOffsetUS := txIndex * (1_000_000 / (rateHz * numTXNodes))\n\n\t// Apply the shift\n\tnewOffsetUS := baseOffsetUS + shiftUS\n\n\t// Ensure we don't exceed the period\n\tmaxOffsetUS := 1_000_000 / rateHz\n\tif newOffsetUS >= maxOffsetUS {\n\t\tnewOffsetUS = newOffsetUS % maxOffsetUS\n\t}\n\n\treturn newOffsetUS\n}\n\n// GetRestaggerOffsets generates new stagger offsets for all TX nodes\n// Returns a map of MAC address to tx_slot_us value\nfunc GetRestaggerOffsets(txMACs []string, rateHz int) map[string]int {\n\tnumTX := len(txMACs)\n\toffsets := make(map[string]int)\n\n\tfor i, mac := range txMACs {\n\t\toffsets[mac] = GenerateRestaggerOffset(i, numTX, rateHz)\n\t}\n\n\treturn offsets\n}\n","numLines":438,"startLine":1,"totalLines":438}}}

!tokenOK {\n508\t\t\t\tif !deadline.IsZero() && time.Now().Before(deadline) {\n509\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s connected without valid token (migration window open until %s)\",\n510\t\t\t\t\t\thello.MAC, deadline.Format(time.RFC3339))\n511\t\t\t\t\tnc.Unpaired = true\n512\t\t\t\t} else {\n513\t\t\t\t\tif hello.Token == \"\" {\n514\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s rejected: missing token\", hello.MAC)\n515\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n516\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s rejected: invalid token\", hello.MAC)\n517\t\t\t\t\t}\n518\t\t\t\t\ts.sendReject(conn, \"invalid_token\")\n519\t\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n520\t\t\t\t\treturn\n521\t\t\t\t}\n522\t\t\t}\n523\t\t}\n524\t\n525\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n526\t\tif existing, exists := s.connections[hello.MAC]; exists {\n527\t\t\texisting.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n528\t\t}\n529\t\ts.connections[hello.MAC] = nc\n530\t\ts.malformedCounts[hello.MAC] = &malformedCounter{}\n531\t\tbroadcaster := s.dashboardBroadcaster\n532\t\tfleetFn := s.fleetNotifier\n533\t\tapDet := s.apDetector\n534\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n535\t\n536\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Node {\n541\t\t\tif err := apDet.ProcessHello(hello.MAC, hello.APBSSID, hello.APChannel); err != nil {\n542\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] AP detector process hello failed: %v\", DefaultVarianceThreshold, \"\")\n555\t\t}\n556\t\n557\t\t// Notify OTA manager of reconnection (for rollback detection)\n558\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n559\t\totaH := s.otaHandler\n560\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n561\t\tif otaH != nil {\n562\t\t\totaH.OnNodeReconnected(hello.MAC, hello.FirmwareVersion)\n563\t\t}\n564\t\n565\t\tgo s.pingLoop(nc)\n566\t\ts.handleMessages(nc)\n567\t}\n568\t\n569\t// handleMessages processes incoming WebSocket messages\n570\tfunc (s *Server) handleMessages(nc *NodeConnection) {\n571\t\tdefer func() {\n572\t\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n573\t\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n574\t\t\tdelete(s.connections, nc.MAC)\n575\t\t\tdelete(s.malformedCounts, nc.MAC)\n576\t\t\tbroadcaster := {\n587\t\t\t\trateCtrl.OnNodeDisconnected(nc.MAC)\n588\t\t\t}\n589\t\t\tif fleetFn != nil {\n590\t\t\t\tfleetFn.OnNodeDisconnected(nc.MAC)\n591\t\t\t}\n592\t\t}()\n593\t\n594\t\tfor {\n595\t\t\tnc.Conn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(readDeadline))\n596\t\n597\t\t\tmessageType, data, err := nc.Conn.ReadMessage()\n598\t\t\tif err != nil {\n599\t\t\t\tif websocket.IsUnexpectedCloseError(err, websocket.CloseGoingAway, websocket.CloseAbnormalClosure) {\n600\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Unexpected close from %s: %v\", nc.MAC, websocket.TextMessage {\n608\t\t\t\ts.handleJSONMessage(nc, data)\n609\t\t\t}\n610\t\t}\n611\t}\n612\t\n613\t// handleBinaryFrame processes a CSI binary frame\n614\tfunc (s *Server) handleBinaryFrame(nc *NodeConnection, data []byte) {\n615\t\t// Load shedding Level 3: drop frames when ingest channel > 50% full.\n616\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n617\t\tsh := s.shedder\n618\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n619\t\tif sh != nil && sh.ShouldDropFrames() {\n620\t\t\treturn\n621\t\t}\n622\t\n623\t\tframe, err := ParseFrame(data)\n624\t\tif err != nil {\n625\t\t\ts.recordMalformed(nc.MAC)\n626\t\t\treturn\n627\t\t}\n628\t\n629\t\tnc.LastFrameTime = time.Now()\n630\t\trecvTime := nc.LastFrameTime\n631\t\n632\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n633\t\treplay := s.replayStore\n634\t\trec := s.recorder\n635\t\tpm := s.processorMgr\n636\t\tcd := s.collisionDetector\n637\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n638\t\n639\t\t// 1. Record raw frame to disk before any processing.\n640\t\t// Load shedding Level 2+: suspend CSI replay buffer writes.\n641\t\tif replay != nil && (sh == nil || sh.ShouldWriteReplay()) {\n642\t\t\tif err := replay.Append(recvTime.UnixNano(), data); err != nil {\n643\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Replay append error: %v\", err)\n644\t\t\t}\n645\t\t}\n646\t\tif rec != nil {\n647\t\t\trec.Write(frame.LinkID(), data)\n648\t\t}\n649\t\n650\t\t// Record frame arrival for collision detection (TX node is peer_mac)\n651\t\tif cd != nil {\n652\t\t\t// The TX node is the peer_mac (the transmitter)\n653\t\t\ttxMAC := frame.PeerMACString()\n654\t\t\tcd.RecordFrameArrival(txMAC, frame.LinkID(), recvTime)\n655\t\t}\n656\t\n657\t\t// 2. Get or create ring buffer.\n658\t\tlinkID := frame.LinkID()\n659\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n660\t\tring, exists := s.links[linkID]\n661\t\tisNewLink := !exists\n662\t\tif !exists {\n663\t\t\tring = NewRingBuffer()\n664\t\t\ts.links[linkID] = ring\n665\t\t}\n666\t\tbroadcaster := s.dashboardBroadcaster\n667\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n668\t\n669\t\tring.Push(frame, recvTime)\n670\t\n671\t\tif broadcaster != nil {\n672\t\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastCSI(frame.MACString(), frame.PeerMACString(), data)\n673\t\t\tif isNewLink {\n674\t\t\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastLinkActive(linkID, frame.MACString(), frame.PeerMACString())\n675\t\t\t}\n676\t\t}\n677\t\n678\t\t// 3. Signal processing pipeline.\n679\t\tif pm != nil && int(frame.NSub) > 0 {\n680\t\t\tresult, err := pm.Process(linkID, frame.Payload, frame.RSSI, int(frame.NSub), recvTime)\n681\t\t\tif err != nil {\n682\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Signal processing error for %s: %v\", linkID, err)\n683\t\t\t\treturn\n684\t\t\t}\n685\t\n686\t\t\tmotionDetected := result.Features.MotionDetected\n687\t\t\tdeltaRMS := result.Features.SmoothDeltaRMS\n688\t\n689\t\t\t// Check if motion state changed.\n690\t\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n691\t\t\tprev := s.linkMotionState[linkID]\n692\t\t\tstateChanged := prev != motionDetected\n693\t\t\ts.linkMotionState[linkID] = motionDetected\n694\t\t\ts.linkDeltaRMS[linkID] = deltaRMS\n695\t\t\tmb := s.motionBroadcaster\n696\t\t\trateCtrl := s.rateCtrl\n697\t\t\teb := s.eventBroadcaster\n698\t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n699\t\n700\t\t\tif stateChanged {\n701\t\t\t\tif mb != nil {\n702\t\t\t\t\tmb.BroadcastMotionState([]MotionStateItem{{\n703\t\t\t\t\t\tLinkID:         linkID,\n704\t\t\t\t\t\tMotionDetected: motionDetected,\n705\t\t\t\t\t\tDeltaRMS:       deltaRMS,\n706\t\t\t\t\t}})\n707\t\t\t\t}\n708\t\t\t\t// Broadcast presence transition event to dashboard.\n709\t\t\t\tif eb != nil {\n710\t\t\t\t\teb.BroadcastEvent(\n711\t\t\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"presence:%s:%d\", linkID, time.Now().UnixMilli()),\n712\t\t\t\t\t\ttime.Now(),\n713\t\t\t\t\t\t\"presence_transition\",\n714\t\t\t\t\t\tlinkID,\n715\t\t\t\t\t\t0,\n716\t\t\t\t\t\t\"\",\n717\t\t\t\t\t)\n718\t\t\t\t}\n719\t\t\t}\n720\t\n721\t\t\tif rateCtrl != nil {\n722\t\t\t\trateCtrl.OnMotionState(nc.MAC, motionDetected)\n723\t\t\t}\n724\t\t}\n725\t}\n726\t\n727\t// handleJSONMessage processes a JSON control message\n728\tfunc (s *Server) handleJSONMessage(nc *NodeConnection, data []byte) {\n729\t\tparsed, err := ParseJSONMessage(data)\n730\t\tif err != nil {\n731\t\t\treturn\n732\t\t}\n733\t\n734\t\tswitch msg := parsed.(type) {\n735\t\tcase *HealthMessage:\n736\t\t\tnc.LastHealth = msg\n737\t\t\tnc.LastHealthTime = time.Now()\n738\t\n739\t\tcase *BLEMessage:\n740\t\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n741\t\t\thandler := recordMalformed tracks malformed frames and closes connection if threshold exceeded\n771\tfunc (s *Server) recordMalformed(mac string) {\n772\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n773\t\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n774\t\n775\t\tcounter, exists := s.malformedCounts[mac]\n776\t\tif !exists {\n777\t\t\treturn\n778\t\t}\n779\t\n780\t\t// Log at DEBUG level for each validation failure\n781\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Node %s sent malformed CSI frame (count in window: %d)\", mac, counter.count+1)\n782\t\n783\t\t// Reset counter if window has expired (sliding 60-second window)\n784\t\tif time.Since(counter.firstSeen) > malformedWindow {\n785\t\t\tcounter.count = 0\n786\t\t\tcounter.firstSeen = time.Now()\n787\t\t}\n788\t\n789\t\tcounter.count++\n790\t\n791\t\t// Log WARN when count exceeds 100 within the window\n792\t\tif counter.count > malformedWarnThreshold && counter.count <= malformedWarnThreshold+1 {\n793\t\t\t// Only log once when crossing the threshold to avoid spam\n794\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s sent %d malformed frames in 60s\", mac, counter.count)\n795\t\t}\n796\t\n797\t\t// Close connection when count exceeds 1000 within the window\n798\t\tif counter.count > malformedCloseThreshold {\n799\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[ERROR] Node %s sent %d malformed frames in 60s — closing connection: Excessive malformed frames — possible firmware bug\", mac, counter.count)\n800\t\t\tif nc, exists := s.connections[mac]; exists {\n801\t\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n802\t\t\t\t// Send close message with specific error text\n803\t\t\t\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage,\n804\t\t\t\t\twebsocket.FormatCloseMessage(websocket.ClosePolicyViolation, \"Excessive malformed frames — possible firmware bug\"))\n805\t\t\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n806\t\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n807\t\t\t}\n808\t\t}\n809\t}\n810\t\n811\t// pingLoop sends periodic ping frames to keep the connection alive\n812\tfunc (s *Server) pingLoop(nc *NodeConnection) {\n813\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(pingInterval)\n814\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n815\t\n816\t\tfor range ticker.C {\n817\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n818\t\t\terr := nc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.PingMessage, nil)\n819\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n820\t\n821\t\t\tif err != nil {\n822\t\t\t\treturn\n823\t\t\t}\n824\t\n825\t\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n826\t\t\tshutdown := s.shutdown\n827\t\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n828\t\t\tif shutdown {\n829\t\t\t\treturn\n830\t\t\t}\n831\t\t}\n832\t}\n833\t\n834\t// sendReject sends a reject message and closes the connection\n835\tfunc (s *Server) sendReject(conn *websocket.Conn, reason string) Ingestion server set to shutting down (HTTP 503 for new connections)\")\n880\t}\n881\t\n882\t// Shutdown gracefully shuts down the server\n883\tfunc (s *Server) Shutdown(ctx context.Context) {\n884\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n885\t\ts.shutdown = true\n886\t\n887\t\tshutdownMsg := ShutdownMessage{Type: \"shutdown\", ReconnectInMS: 30000}\n888\t\tdata, _ := json.Marshal(shutdownMsg)\n889\t\n890\t\tfor conn.ReadMessage()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Failed to read hello: %v\", err)\n\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tparsed, err := ParseJSONMessage(msg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.sendReject(conn, \"invalid hello format\")\n\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\thello, ok := parsed.(*HelloMessage)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\ts.sendReject(conn, \"expected hello first\")\n\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tnc.MAC = hello.MAC\n\tnc.Hello = hello\n\n\t// Token validation: if a validator is configured, reject unauthenticated nodes\n\t// unless the migration window is still open, in which case allow but mark as Unpaired.\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tvalidator := s.tokenValidator\n\tdeadline := s.migrationDeadline\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\tif validator != nil {\n\t\ttokenOK := hello.Token != \"\" && validator(hello.MAC, hello.Token)\n\t\tif !tokenOK {\n\t\t\tif !deadline.IsZero() && time.Now().Before(deadline) {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s connected without valid token (migration window open until %s)\",\n\t\t\t\t\thello.MAC, deadline.Format(time.RFC3339))\n\t\t\t\tnc.Unpaired = true\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tif hello.Token == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s rejected: missing token\", hello.MAC)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s rejected: invalid token\", hello.MAC)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\ts.sendReject(conn, \"invalid_token\")\n\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tif existing, exists := s.connections[hello.MAC]; exists {\n\t\texisting.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t}\n\ts.connections[hello.MAC] = nc\n\ts.malformedCounts[hello.MAC] = &malformedCounter{}\n\tbroadcaster := s.dashboardBroadcaster\n\tfleetFn := s.fleetNotifier\n\tapDet := s.apDetector\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Node connected: MAC=%s firmware=%s chip=%s\",\n\t\thello.MAC, hello.FirmwareVersion, hello.Chip)\n\n\t// Process AP BSSID for passive radar auto-detection\n\tif apDet != nil {\n\t\tif err := apDet.ProcessHello(hello.MAC, hello.APBSSID, hello.APChannel); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] AP detector process hello failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif broadcaster != nil {\n\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastNodeConnected(hello.MAC, hello.FirmwareVersion, hello.Chip, nc.Unpaired)\n\t}\n\n\tif fleetFn != nil {\n\t\tfleetFn.OnNodeConnected(hello.MAC, hello.FirmwareVersion, hello.Chip)\n\t} else {\n\t\ts.sendRole(nc, \"rx\", \"\")\n\t\ts.sendConfig(nc, RateIdle, 0, DefaultVarianceThreshold, \"\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Notify OTA manager of reconnection (for rollback detection)\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\totaH := s.otaHandler\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\tif otaH != nil {\n\t\totaH.OnNodeReconnected(hello.MAC, hello.FirmwareVersion)\n\t}\n\n\tgo s.pingLoop(nc)\n\ts.handleMessages(nc)\n}\n\n// handleMessages processes incoming WebSocket messages\nfunc (s *Server) handleMessages(nc *NodeConnection) {\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\tdelete(s.connections, nc.MAC)\n\t\tdelete(s.malformedCounts, nc.MAC)\n\t\tbroadcaster := s.dashboardBroadcaster\n\t\trateCtrl := s.rateCtrl\n\t\tfleetFn := s.fleetNotifier\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Node disconnected: MAC=%s\", nc.MAC)\n\n\t\tif broadcaster != nil {\n\t\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastNodeDisconnected(nc.MAC)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif rateCtrl != nil {\n\t\t\trateCtrl.OnNodeDisconnected(nc.MAC)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif fleetFn != nil {\n\t\t\tfleetFn.OnNodeDisconnected(nc.MAC)\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tnc.Conn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(readDeadline))\n\n\t\tmessageType, data, err := nc.Conn.ReadMessage()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tif websocket.IsUnexpectedCloseError(err, websocket.CloseGoingAway, websocket.CloseAbnormalClosure) {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Unexpected close from %s: %v\", nc.MAC, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif messageType == websocket.BinaryMessage {\n\t\t\ts.handleBinaryFrame(nc, data)\n\t\t} else if messageType == websocket.TextMessage {\n\t\t\ts.handleJSONMessage(nc, data)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleBinaryFrame processes a CSI binary frame\nfunc (s *Server) handleBinaryFrame(nc *NodeConnection, data []byte) {\n\t// Load shedding Level 3: drop frames when ingest channel > 50% full.\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tsh := s.shedder\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\tif sh != nil && sh.ShouldDropFrames() {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tframe, err := ParseFrame(data)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.recordMalformed(nc.MAC)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tnc.LastFrameTime = time.Now()\n\trecvTime := nc.LastFrameTime\n\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\treplay := s.replayStore\n\trec := s.recorder\n\tpm := s.processorMgr\n\tcd := s.collisionDetector\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// 1. Record raw frame to disk before any processing.\n\t// Load shedding Level 2+: suspend CSI replay buffer writes.\n\tif replay != nil && (sh == nil || sh.ShouldWriteReplay()) {\n\t\tif err := replay.Append(recvTime.UnixNano(), data); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Replay append error: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif rec != nil {\n\t\trec.Write(frame.LinkID(), data)\n\t}\n\n\t// Record frame arrival for collision detection (TX node is peer_mac)\n\tif cd != nil {\n\t\t// The TX node is the peer_mac (the transmitter)\n\t\ttxMAC := frame.PeerMACString()\n\t\tcd.RecordFrameArrival(txMAC, frame.LinkID(), recvTime)\n\t}\n\n\t// 2. Get or create ring buffer.\n\tlinkID := frame.LinkID()\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tring, exists := s.links[linkID]\n\tisNewLink := !exists\n\tif !exists {\n\t\tring = NewRingBuffer()\n\t\ts.links[linkID] = ring\n\t}\n\tbroadcaster := s.dashboardBroadcaster\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tring.Push(frame, recvTime)\n\n\tif broadcaster != nil {\n\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastCSI(frame.MACString(), frame.PeerMACString(), data)\n\t\tif isNewLink {\n\t\t\tbroadcaster.BroadcastLinkActive(linkID, frame.MACString(), frame.PeerMACString())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// 3. Signal processing pipeline.\n\tif pm != nil && int(frame.NSub) > 0 {\n\t\tresult, err := pm.Process(linkID, frame.Payload, frame.RSSI, int(frame.NSub), recvTime)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Signal processing error for %s: %v\", linkID, err)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmotionDetected := result.Features.MotionDetected\n\t\tdeltaRMS := result.Features.SmoothDeltaRMS\n\n\t\t// Check if motion state changed.\n\t\ts.mu.Lock()\n\t\tprev := s.linkMotionState[linkID]\n\t\tstateChanged := prev != motionDetected\n\t\ts.linkMotionState[linkID] = motionDetected\n\t\ts.linkDeltaRMS[linkID] = deltaRMS\n\t\tmb := s.motionBroadcaster\n\t\trateCtrl := s.rateCtrl\n\t\teb := s.eventBroadcaster\n\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\tif stateChanged {\n\t\t\tif mb != nil {\n\t\t\t\tmb.BroadcastMotionState([]MotionStateItem{{\n\t\t\t\t\tLinkID:         linkID,\n\t\t\t\t\tMotionDetected: motionDetected,\n\t\t\t\t\tDeltaRMS:       deltaRMS,\n\t\t\t\t}})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Broadcast presence transition event to dashboard.\n\t\t\tif eb != nil {\n\t\t\t\teb.BroadcastEvent(\n\t\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"presence:%s:%d\", linkID, time.Now().UnixMilli()),\n\t\t\t\t\ttime.Now(),\n\t\t\t\t\t\"presence_transition\",\n\t\t\t\t\tlinkID,\n\t\t\t\t\t0,\n\t\t\t\t\t\"\",\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif rateCtrl != nil {\n\t\t\trateCtrl.OnMotionState(nc.MAC, motionDetected)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleJSONMessage processes a JSON control message\nfunc (s *Server) handleJSONMessage(nc *NodeConnection, data []byte) {\n\tparsed, err := ParseJSONMessage(data)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tswitch msg := parsed.(type) {\n\tcase *HealthMessage:\n\t\tnc.LastHealth = msg\n\t\tnc.LastHealthTime = time.Now()\n\n\tcase *BLEMessage:\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\thandler := s.bleHandler\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\t\tif handler != nil {\n\t\t\thandler(nc.MAC, msg.Devices)\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase *MotionHintMessage:\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\trateCtrl := s.rateCtrl\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\t\tif rateCtrl != nil {\n\t\t\trateCtrl.OnMotionHint(nc.MAC)\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase *OTAStatusMessage:\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] OTA %s from %s: state=%s progress=%d%%\",\n\t\t\tmsg.Type, nc.MAC, msg.State, msg.ProgressPct)\n\t\tif msg.Error != \"\" {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] OTA error from %s: %s\", nc.MAC, msg.Error)\n\t\t}\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\totaH := s.otaHandler\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\t\tif otaH != nil {\n\t\t\totaH.OnOTAStatus(nc.MAC, msg.State, uint8(msg.ProgressPct), msg.Error)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// recordMalformed tracks malformed frames and closes connection if threshold exceeded\nfunc (s *Server) recordMalformed(mac string) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tcounter, exists := s.malformedCounts[mac]\n\tif !exists {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Log at DEBUG level for each validation failure\n\tlog.Printf(\"[DEBUG] Node %s sent malformed CSI frame (count in window: %d)\", mac, counter.count+1)\n\n\t// Reset counter if window has expired (sliding 60-second window)\n\tif time.Since(counter.firstSeen) > malformedWindow {\n\t\tcounter.count = 0\n\t\tcounter.firstSeen = time.Now()\n\t}\n\n\tcounter.count++\n\n\t// Log WARN when count exceeds 100 within the window\n\tif counter.count > malformedWarnThreshold && counter.count <= malformedWarnThreshold+1 {\n\t\t// Only log once when crossing the threshold to avoid spam\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[WARN] Node %s sent %d malformed frames in 60s\", mac, counter.count)\n\t}\n\n\t// Close connection when count exceeds 1000 within the window\n\tif counter.count > malformedCloseThreshold {\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[ERROR] Node %s sent %d malformed frames in 60s — closing connection: Excessive malformed frames — possible firmware bug\", mac, counter.count)\n\t\tif nc, exists := s.connections[mac]; exists {\n\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\t\t\t// Send close message with specific error text\n\t\t\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage,\n\t\t\t\twebsocket.FormatCloseMessage(websocket.ClosePolicyViolation, \"Excessive malformed frames — possible firmware bug\"))\n\t\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// pingLoop sends periodic ping frames to keep the connection alive\nfunc (s *Server) pingLoop(nc *NodeConnection) {\n\tticker := time.NewTicker(pingInterval)\n\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\n\tfor range ticker.C {\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\t\terr := nc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.PingMessage, nil)\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ts.mu.RLock()\n\t\tshutdown := s.shutdown\n\t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\t\tif shutdown {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// sendReject sends a reject message and closes the connection\nfunc (s *Server) sendReject(conn *websocket.Conn, reason string) {\n\tmsg := RejectMessage{Type: \"reject\", Reason: reason}\n\tdata, _ := json.Marshal(msg)\n\tconn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, data)\n}\n\n// sendRole sends a role assignment to a node\nfunc (s *Server) sendRole(nc *NodeConnection, role string, passiveBSSID string) {\n\tmsg := RoleMessage{Type: \"role\", Role: role, PassiveBSSID: passiveBSSID}\n\tdata, _ := json.Marshal(msg)\n\n\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, data)\n\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n}\n\n// sendConfig sends configuration to a node\nfunc (s *Server) sendConfig(nc *NodeConnection, rateHz int, txSlotUS int, varianceThreshold float64, ntpServer string) {\n\tmsg := ConfigMessage{Type: \"config\"}\n\tif rateHz > 0 {\n\t\tmsg.RateHz = &rateHz\n\t}\n\tif txSlotUS > 0 {\n\t\tmsg.TXSlotUS = &txSlotUS\n\t}\n\tif varianceThreshold > 0 {\n\t\tmsg.VarianceThreshold = &varianceThreshold\n\t}\n\tif ntpServer != \"\" {\n\t\tmsg.NTPServer = &ntpServer\n\t}\n\tdata, _ := json.Marshal(msg)\n\n\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, data)\n\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n}\n\n// SetShuttingDown sets the shutdown flag. This causes HandleNodeWS to return HTTP 503\n// for new connection attempts. Called as step 1 of the graceful shutdown sequence.\nfunc (s *Server) SetShuttingDown() {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\ts.shutdown = true\n\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Ingestion server set to shutting down (HTTP 503 for new connections)\")\n}\n\n// Shutdown gracefully shuts down the server\nfunc (s *Server) Shutdown(ctx context.Context) {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\ts.shutdown = true\n\n\tshutdownMsg := ShutdownMessage{Type: \"shutdown\", ReconnectInMS: 30000}\n\tdata, _ := json.Marshal(shutdownMsg)\n\n\tfor mac, nc := range s.connections {\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\t\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, data)\n\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n\t\tdelete(s.connections, mac)\n\t}\n\ts.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] Ingestion server shutdown complete\")\n}\n\n// CloseAllConnections closes all node WebSocket connections with normal close frame.\n// This implements the shutdown.NodeConnectionCloser interface.\nfunc (s *Server) CloseAllConnections() error {\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tfor mac, nc := range s.connections {\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Lock()\n\t\t// Send normal close frame (1000)\n\t\tnc.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage,\n\t\t\twebsocket.FormatCloseMessage(websocket.CloseNormalClosure, \"mothership shutting down\"))\n\t\tnc.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\tnc.writeMu.Unlock()\n\t\tdelete(s.connections, mac)\n\t}\n\tlog.Printf(\"[INFO] All node connections closed\")\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetConnectedNodes returns a list of connected node MACs\nfunc (s *Server) GetConnectedNodes() []string {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tmacs := make([]string, 0, len(s.connections))\n\tfor mac := range s.connections {\n\t\tmacs = append(macs, mac)\n\t}\n\treturn macs\n}\n\n// NodeInfo represents a connected node's state for dashboard\ntype NodeInfo struct {\n\tMAC             string `json:\"mac\"`\n\tFirmwareVersion string `json:\"firmware_version,omitempty\"`\n\tChip            string `json:\"chip,omitempty\"`\n\tUnpaired        bool   `json:\"unpaired,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// GetConnectedNodesInfo returns detailed info about connected nodes\nfunc (s *Server) GetConnectedNodesInfo() []NodeInfo {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tnodes := make([]NodeInfo, 0, len(s.connections))\n\tfor mac, nc := range s.connections {\n\t\tinfo := NodeInfo{MAC: mac, Unpaired: nc.Unpaired}\n\t\tif nc.Hello != nil {\n\t\t\tinfo.FirmwareVersion = nc.Hello.FirmwareVersion\n\t\t\tinfo.Chip = nc.Hello.Chip\n\t\t}\n\t\tnodes = append(nodes, info)\n\t}\n\treturn nodes\n}\n\n// GetUnpairedMACs returns the MACs of currently-connected nodes that lack a valid token.\nfunc (s *Server) GetUnpairedMACs() []string {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tvar macs []string\n\tfor mac, nc := range s.connections {\n\t\tif nc.Unpaired {\n\t\t\tmacs = append(macs, mac)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn macs\n}\n\n// LinkInfo represents a link with its endpoints and health data\ntype LinkInfo struct {\n\tID         string  `json:\"id\"`\n\tNodeMAC    string  `json:\"node_mac\"`\n\tPeerMAC    string  `json:\"peer_mac\"`\n\tHealthScore float64 `json:\"health_score,omitempty\"` // Ambient confidence score (0-1)\n\t// Alias fields for frontend compatibility with proactive.js\n\tCompositeScore float64 `json:\"composite_score,omitempty\"` // Alias for HealthScore\n\tQuality        float64 `json:\"quality,omitempty\"`        // Alias for HealthScore\n\tLinkID         string  `json:\"link_id,omitempty\"`         // Alias for ID\n}\n\n// LinkHealthInfo represents a link with health metrics for the API response\ntype LinkHealthInfo struct {\n\tLinkID        string               `json:\"link_id\"`\n\tTXMAC         string               `json:\"tx_mac\"`\n\tRXMAC         string               `json:\"rx_mac\"`\n\tHealthScore   float64              `json:\"health_score\"`\n\tHealthDetails signal.HealthDetails `json:\"health_details\"`\n\tLastUpdated   time.Time            `json:\"last_updated\"`\n}\n\n// GetAllLinksInfo returns detailed info about all active links\nfunc (s *Server) GetAllLinksInfo() []LinkInfo {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tpm := s.processorMgr\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\ts.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tlinks := make([]LinkInfo, 0, len(s.links))\n\tfor linkID := range s.links {\n\t\tif len(linkID) >= 35 {\n\t\t\tinfo := LinkInfo{\n\t\t\t\tID:      linkID,\n\t\t\t\tNodeMAC: linkID[:17],\n\t\t\t\tPeerMAC: linkID[18:],\n\t\t\t\tLinkID:  linkID, // Alias for frontend\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Get health score from processor manager if available\n\t\t\tif pm != nil {\n\t\t\t\tif proc := pm.GetProcessor(linkID); proc != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tif health := proc.GetHealth(); health != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tinfo.HealthScore = health.GetAmbientConfidence()\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// Populate alias fields for frontend compatibility\n\t\t\t\t\t\tinfo.CompositeScore = info.HealthScore\n\t\t\t\t\t\tinfo.Quality = info.HealthScore\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlinks = append(links, info)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn links\n}\n\n// GetAllMotionStates returns current motion state for all known links.\nfunc (s *Server) GetAllMotionStates() []MotionStateItem {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tpm := s.processorMgr\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tstates := make([]MotionStateItem, 0, len(s.linkMotionState))\n\tfor linkID, detected := range s.linkMotionState {\n\t\titem := MotionStateItem{\n\t\t\tLinkID:         linkID,\n\t\t\tMotionDetected: detected,\n\t\t\tDeltaRMS:       s.linkDeltaRMS[linkID],\n\t\t}\n\t\tif pm != nil {\n\t\t\tif proc := pm.GetProcessor(linkID); proc != nil {\n\t\t\t\titem.Confidence = proc.GetBaseline().GetConfidence()\n\t\t\t\titem.DiurnalConfidence = proc.GetDiurnal().GetOverallConfidence()\n\t\t\t\titem.DiurnalReady = proc.GetDiurnal().IsReady()\n\t\t\t\t// Phase 6: Add breathing/dwell state\n\t\t\t\tdwellState := proc.GetDwellState()\n\t\t\t\titem.BreathingState = dwellState.String()\n\t\t\t\tbpm := proc.GetDwellBreathingRate()\n\t\t\t\tif bpm > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\titem.BreathingBPM = bpm\n\t\t\t\t\t// Breathing frequency in Hz (for compatibility)\n\t\t\t\t\tfreqHz := bpm / 60.0\n\t\t\t\t\titem.BreathingFreqHz = &freqHz\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tstates = append(states, item)\n\t}\n\treturn states\n}\n\n// GetLinkBuffer returns the ring buffer for a specific link\nfunc (s *Server) GetLinkBuffer(nodeMAC, peerMAC string) *RingBuffer {\n\tlinkID := nodeMAC + \":\" + peerMAC\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n\treturn s.links[linkID]\n}\n\n// GetAllLinksWithHealth returns all links with their health metrics\nfunc (s *Server) GetAllLinksWithHealth() []LinkHealthInfo {\n\ts.mu.RLock()\n\tpm := s.processorMgr\n\tlinks := make([]string, 0, len(s.links))\n\tfor linkID := range s.links {\n\t\tlinks = append(links, linkID)\n\t}\n\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tresult := make([]LinkHealthInfo, 0, len(links))\n\tfor _, linkID := range links {\n\t\tif len(linkID) < 35 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tinfo := LinkHealthInfo{\n\t\t\tLinkID: linkID,\n\t\t\tTXMAC:  linkID[:17],\n\t\t\tRXMAC:  linkID[18:],\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif pm != nil {\n\t\t\tif proc := pm.GetProcessor(linkID); proc != nil {\n\t\t\t\thealth := proc.GetHealth()\n\t\t\t\tif health != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tinfo.HealthScore = health.GetAmbientConfidence()\n\t\t\t\t\tinfo.HealthDetails = health.GetHealthDetails()\n\t\t\t\t\tinfo.LastUpdated = time.Now()\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Default health if not available\n\t\tif info.HealthScore == 0 && info.HealthDetails == (signal.HealthDetails{}) {\n\t\t\tinfo.HealthScore = 0.5\n\t\t\tinfo.HealthDetails = signal.HealthDetails{\n\t\t\t\tSNR:           0.5,\n\t\t\t\tPhaseStability: 0.5,\n\t\t\t\tPacketRate:
